CHOer/GXcs8KYxRPRgMBoPBYDAYDAaDwWVizqMNBoPBYDAYDAaDwWBwmRijejAYDAaDwWAwGAwGg8vEGNWDwWAwGAwGg8FgMBhcJsaoHgwGg8FgMBgMBoPB4DIxRvVgMBgMBoPBYDAYDAaXiTGqB4PBYDAYDAaDwWAwuEyMUT0YDAaDwWAwGAwGg8FlYozqwWAwGAwGg8FgMBgMLhNjVA8Gg8FgMBgMBoPBYHCZGKN6MBgMBoPBYDAYDAaDy8QY1YPBYDAYDAaDwWAwGFwmxqgeDAaDwWAwGAwGg8HgMjFG9WAwGAwGg8FgMBgMBpeJMaoHg8FgMBgMBoPBYDC4TIxRPRgMBoPBYDAYDAaDwWVijOrBYDAYDAaDwWAwGAwuCwcH/z/v+XN6dElWAwAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==)


"""

import heapq

assumption = {
    "Arad": "A", "Bucharest": "Z", "Craiova": "S", "Eforie": "T",
    "Fagaras": "O", "Dobreta": "V", "Hirsova": "N", "Iasi": "Q",


    "Neamt": "F", "Oradea": "B", "Pitesti": "P", "RimnicuVilcea": "R",
    "Timisoara": "C", "Urziceni": "D", "Vaslui": "H", "Zerind": "E",
    "Lugoj": "G", "Mehadia": "L", "Sibiu": "Sibiu", "Giurgiu": "Giurgiu"
}

heuristic = {}
neighbors = {}
#=========================================================
def taking_data(file_path):
    start = None
    goal = None
    with open(file_path, "r") as file:
        for line in file:
            parts = line.split()
            current_node = assumption.get(parts[0])

            if start is None:
                start = current_node
            heuristic[current_node] = int(parts[1])
            if heuristic[current_node] == 0:
                goal = current_node

            neighbors[current_node] = []
            for i in range(2, len(parts), 2):
                neighbor_node = assumption.get(parts[i])
                distance = int(parts[i + 1])
                neighbors[current_node].append((neighbor_node, distance))

    return start, goal
#=========================================================
def a_star(start, goal, heuristic, neighbors):
    open_set = [(0, start)]
    came_from = {}
    cost_so_far = {start: 0}

    while open_set:
        current_cost, current = heapq.heappop(open_set)

        if current == goal:
            break

        for neighbor, move_cost in neighbors.get(current, []):
            new_cost = cost_so_far[current] + move_cost

            if neighbor not in cost_so_far or new_cost < cost_so_far[neighbor]:
                cost_so_far[neighbor] = new_cost
                priority = new_cost + heuristic.get(neighbor, float('inf'))
                heapq.heappush(open_set, (priority, neighbor))
                came_from[neighbor] = current

    return came_from, cost_so_far
#=========================================================
def output_generator(came_from, cost, start, goal):
    path = []
    current = goal

    # Trace back to reconstruct the path
    while current != start:
        if current not in came_from:
            print("NO PATH FOUND")
            return
        path.append(current)
        current = came_from[current]
    path.append(start)
    path.reverse()

    # Convert path from abbreviations back to full names
    reverse_assumption = {v: k for k, v in assumption.items()}
    full_path = " -> ".join(reverse_assumption.get(node, f"Unknown({node})") for node in path)

    print(f"Path: {full_path}")
    print(f"Total distance: {cost.get(goal, 'N/A')} km")
#=========================================================
file_path = "input1.txt"
start, goal = taking_data(file_path)
if start is None or goal is None:
    print("NO PATH FOUND")
else:
    came_from, cost = a_star(start, goal, heuristic, neighbors)
    output_generator(came_from, cost, start, goal)
